If you've made the effort to plan small details like escort cards and <a href=\\\"https://www.bridestory.com/blog/all-you-need-to-know-about-boutonnieres-and-corsages\\\" target=\\\"_blank\\\">boutonnieres</a>, why not do the same for your ring bearer pillow?</p><p>Think beyond traditional, poufy ring bearer pillows; these days, ring holders come in different shapes, styles, and sizes. Couples are even opting for fun alternatives like unique ring boxes, antique books, even wood or moss. Below, we've selected 13 creative ring holder ideas for your viewing pleasure. Keep scrolling to see them!</p><p><br></p>\",\"metaKeyword\":\"wedding, creative, weddingideasid, personalized, bridestoryid\",\"homestreamImage\":\"http://images.bridestory.com/image/upload/blogs/1_classic_hyaqqs.jpg\",\"previewImage\":\"http://images.bridestory.com/image/upload/blogs/1_classic_hyaqqs.jpg\",\"primaryImage\":\"http://images.bridestory.com/image/upload/blogs/1_classic_hyaqqs.jpg\",\"createdAt\":\"2017-04-18T09:18:11+00:00\",\"updatedAt\":\"2017-04-20T08:23:58+00:00\",\"publishedAt\":\"2017-04-20T02:00:00+00:00\",\"realWeddingId\":\"0\",\"status\":\"published\",\"authorAlias\":null,\"views\":0,\"metaDescription\":\"\",\"content\":\"<p><b>Classic ring pillow<br></b>First on the list is the classic ring bearer pillow. This option works every time and suits any kind of celebration, from a white wedding to an intimate soirée. An all-white ring pillow never goes out of style, and you can customize it simply by choosing a different color for the ribbon.</p><p><br></p><p style=\\\"text-align: center;\\\"><img src=\\\"http://images.bridestory.com/image/upload/q_80,f_auto/hyhssiddy4q8nlmuv6w3.jpg\\\" data-redactor-inserted-image=\\\"true\\\"><br><em>Photography: Stephanie Reeder Photography - Becky Young</em></p><p><b>Earthy elements<br></b>Outdoor or rustic weddings pair especially well with unique ring holders made of natural elements. Which one do you prefer, a lush moss ring holder or a wooden log tray to hold your wedding rings?</p><p><br></p><p style=\\\"text-align: center;\\\"><img src=\\\"http://images.bridestory.com/image/upload/q_80,f_auto/aef7pdy4mzowyqptvo9n.jpg\\\" data-redactor-inserted-image=\\\"true\\\"><br><em>Photography: MIchelle Carmichael - Raymond Hom</em><span></span><br></p><p><b>Patterned fabrics<br></b>Here's another way to spice up your wedding ring pillow; play around with different fabrics of any color or pattern. Prepare a block-shaped flower cork and push in daisies, baby chrysanthemums, or other puffy flowers to fully cover the cork. The result? A beautiful flower box to tie your rings on.</p><p><br></p><p style=\\\"text-align: center;\\\"><img src=\\\"http://images.bridestory.com/image/upload/q_80,f_auto/fydezre134fhgqipm1jy.jpg\\\" data-redactor-inserted-image=\\\"true\\\"><br><em>Photography: Natalie Watson - Jose Villa</em><span></span><br></p><p><b>Blooming flowers<br></b>This is a great idea for all you romantic brides. Bookworms will especially love the idea of using antique books as ring boxes. You can tie your rings around the book, or cut a box-shaped hole inside an old, unused book instead.</p><p><br></p><p style=\\\"text-align: center;\\\"><img src=\\\"http://images.bridestory.com/image/upload/q_80,f_auto/rckenhpkfbmdqzwkrmtr.jpg\\\" data-redactor-inserted-image=\\\"true\\\"><br><em>Photography: Carrie Patterson Photography - The Grovers</em><span></span><br></p><p><b>Handmade with love<br></b>Crafty brides should not miss out on this sentimental ring pillow idea.
